If the height of a view exceeds the paperheight, there should be no break before (since it will be impossible to fit it in anywhere => an infinite loop). We don't have access to the pageheight here, therefore an "educated guess" is made: No breaks are inserted before views starting within the first 1% (chosen to avoid round-off errors) of the available space given by actBreakHeight. If the view starts after the first 1%, a break is inserted and the view will start at the top of the next page (i.e. withing the first 1% this time).
